</td></tr>

</th>

<span class="expandline" title="16 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_string_ensemble&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring string ensemble</a></span>; <tr>
<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>The set includes 2 copies of Continuo part probably to serve 3 players (violoncello, violone, and harpsichord). Both copies are included here to see more of the composer's manuscripts. Major part of the set was witten by the composer himself with the following exceptions:<br />Violino 1, 1st and 2nd movements: J. L. Krebs<br />Violino 2, 1st and 2nd movements: Anon. L71<br />Continuo (1), 2nd page and later: C. P. E. Bach<br />Continuo (2), 1st and 2nd movements: Anon. L72
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Earliest surviving source is a set of parts copied out ca.1730; believed to have been composed ca.1717–1723 in Cöthen but perhaps composed instead when Bach was in Leipzig.
</p><p>In 1865 an arrangement by Friedrich Hermann "1ière Concerto (Am.) p. Violon av. Pfte arr. p. Fr. Hermann." was published by Peters (Edition Peters no.229, plate 4476, 19 pages score, 7 pages violin part, acc. to <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldcat.org/oclc/223146258">WorldCat</a></span>.) - Schissel
</p>
